     <h2 class="trb_outfit_primaryItem_article_title trb_outfit_featuredArticleTitle">
      <a href="/news/breaking/mc-allentown-girl-takes-south-mountain-loaded-gun-on-campus-20161201-story.html#nt=oft12aH-2la1" class="trb_outfit_primaryItem_article_title_a">
       Girl took loaded gun to Allentown middle school, police say
      </a>

   <p class="trb_outfit_primaryItem_article_content">
    <span class="trb_outfit_primaryItem_article_content_text">
     ALLENTOWN — A South Mountain Middle School student took a loaded gun to school on Thursday, authorities said.   Other students found out about the gun and notified school officials who found the weapon inside the girl&apos;s locker, Assistant Chief Gail Struss said.   The girl was taken into custody and...

   </p>

    <a href="/entertainment/lehigh-valley-music/mc-ladysmith-black-mambazo-blues-brothers-tribute-and-celtic-rockers-enter-the-haggis-set-for-dates-at-20161201-story.html#nt=oft07a-7gp2" class="trb_outfit_relatedListTitle_a">
     Ladysmith Black Mambazo, Blues Brothers tribute and Celtic rockers Enter the Haggis set for dates at Musikfest Cafe
    </a>
    <span class="trb_outfits_metabuckets">
     <span class="trb_outfits_metabuckets_1">
     </span>
    </span>
   </h3>
   <p class="trb_outfit_group_list_item_brief">
    Grammy Award winners Ladysmith Black Mambazo, popular Blues Brothers tribute The Blues Brotherhood and Celtic rock band Enter The Haggis all will perform at Musikfest Cafe at ArtsQuest Center this winter, it was just announced.   Tickets for all the shows will go on sale at 10 a.m. Dec. 6 to ArtsQuest...

  <section class="trb_outfit_primaryItem trb_outfit_section" data-outfits-nexttype="group" data-outfits-lead-art-first="false" data-content-id="92023796" data-content-slug="mc-locktenders-house-restoration-atv-20161201" data-content-section="News" data-content-type="column">
   <article class="trb_outfit_primaryItem_article">
    <div class="trb_outfit_primaryItem_label">
     <span class="trb_outfit_categorySectionHeading">
      <a class="trb_outfit_categorySectionHeading_a" href="/news/local/burbs/#nt=oft02a-12la1">

    <h2 class="trb_outfit_primaryItem_article_title trb_outfit_featuredArticleTitle">
     <a href="/news/local/burbs/mc-locktenders-house-restoration-atv-20161201-column.html#nt=oft02a-12la1" class="trb_outfit_primaryItem_article_title_a">
      Restoration of locktender&apos;s house putting a shine on Lehigh Canal history
     </a>
     <span class="trb_outfits_metabuckets">
      <span class="trb_outfits_metabuckets_1">
      </span>
     </span>
    </h2>
    <div class="trb_bylines">
     <span class="trb_bylines_nm_pm">
      <span data-byline-withoutby="data-byline-withoutby" class="trb_bylines_nm_au">
       Dan Sheehan
      </span>
     </span>
    </div>
   </article>
   <figure class="trb_outfit_primaryItem_leadArt">
    <aside class="trb_embed" data-content-id="92023809" data-content-size="leadart" data-content-type="image" data-content-slug="mc-mch-locktendersrestoration4-20161201" data-content-subtype="photo" data-role="sc_item imgsize_ratiosizecontainer" data-state="">
     <div class="trb_embed_media">
      <a href="/news/local/burbs/mc-locktenders-house-restoration-atv-20161201-column.html#nt=oft02a-12la1" data-role=" delayload  delayload_done imgsize_item" class="trb_embed_imageContainer_figure">
       <img itemprop="image" data-baseurl="http://www.trbimg.com/img-58409570/turbine/mc-mch-locktendersrestoration4-20161201" class="trb_embed_imageContainer_img" data-c-nd="2048x1536" />
      </a>
      <div class="trb_embed_related" data-role="lightbox_metadata">
       <a href="/news/local/burbs/mc-locktenders-house-restoration-atv-20161201-column.html#nt=oft02a-12la1">
       </a>
       <div class="trb_embed_related_credit">
        Delaware &amp; Lehigh National Heritage
       </div>
       <div class="trb_embed_related_caption">
        The Delaware &amp; Lehigh National Heritage Corridor is restoring the locktender’s house in Freemansburg, a stone building along the towpath of the Lehigh Canal. Locktenders once lived there and ran the equipment that raised and lowered anthracite-hauling boats at Lock 44.
       </div>
       <div class="trb_embed_related_credit_and_caption">
        The Delaware &amp; Lehigh National Heritage Corridor is restoring the locktender’s house in Freemansburg, a stone building along the towpath of the Lehigh Canal. Locktenders once lived there and ran the equipment that raised and lowered anthracite-hauling boats at Lock 44. (Delaware &amp; Lehigh National Heritage)
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
    </aside>
   </figure>

    <h3 class="trb_outfit_relatedListTitle">
     <a href="/business/players/mc-new-hire-play-1202-20161201-story.html#nt=oft13a-21gp1" class="trb_outfit_relatedListTitle_a">
      Drew Diskin has joined Health Network Laboratories as senior vice president of business development
     </a>
     <span class="trb_outfits_metabuckets">
      <span class="trb_outfits_metabuckets_1">
      </span>
     </span>
    </h3>
   </section>
   <p class="trb_outfit_group_list_item_brief">
    DREW DISKIN   Diskin has joined Health Network Laboratories as senior vice president of business development.   Prior to joining HNL, Diskin was vice president and chief marketing officer at WizeHive – a database management software company focusing on nonprofits and health care. He also previously...
